<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification (CONCACAF)</h1>
<div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">

<p>The North, Central American and Caribbean section of the <b><a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification</a></b> acts as qualifiers for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>, to be held in Russia, for national teams which are members of the <a href="/wiki/CONCACAF" title="CONCACAF">Confederation of North, Central American and Caribbean Association Football</a> (CONCACAF). A total of 3.5 slots (3 direct slots and 1 inter-confederation play-off slot) in the final tournament are available for CONCACAF teams.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-1"><a href="#cite_note-1">[1]</a></sup></p>
<p>In a change to previous qualification tournaments for this confederation,<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> the first three rounds will be played as knockout rounds, with both the fourth round and the final round (referred to as 'The Hexagonal') played as group stages. The first round was played during the FIFA international dates of 23–31 March 2015.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-3"><a href="#cite_note-3">[3]</a></sup> CONCACAF announced the full format details on 12 January 2015.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-approval_4-0"><a href="#cite_note-approval-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-si_5-0"><a href="#cite_note-si-5">[5]</a></sup></p>
<p></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Format">Format</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONCACAF)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Format">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>The qualification structure is as follows:<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-approval_4-1"><a href="#cite_note-approval-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup></p>
<ul>
<li><b>First round</b>: A total of 14 teams (teams ranked 22–35) played home-and-away over <a href="/wiki/Two-legged_tie" title="Two-legged tie">two legs</a>. The seven winners advanced to the second round.</li>
<li><b>Second round</b>: A total of 20 teams (teams ranked 9–21 and seven first round winners) played home-and-away over two legs. The ten winners advanced to the third round.</li>
<li><b>Third round</b>: A total of 12 teams (teams ranked 7–8 and ten second round winners) played home-and-away over two legs. The six winners advanced to the fourth round.</li>
<li><b>Fourth round</b>: A total of 12 teams (teams ranked 1–6 and six third round winners) were divided into three groups of four teams to play home-and-away <a href="/wiki/Round-robin_tournament" title="Round-robin tournament">round-robin</a> matches. The top two teams of each group advanced to the fifth round.</li>
<li><b>Fifth round</b>: The six teams which advance from the fourth round will play home-and-away round-robin matches in one single group (often referred to as the "Hexagonal"). The top three teams will qualify for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a>, and the fourth-placed team will advance to the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(inter-confederation_play-offs)" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification (inter-confederation play-offs)">inter-confederation play-offs</a>.</li>
</ul>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Entrants">Entrants</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONCACAF)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Entrants">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>All 35 FIFA-affiliated national teams from CONCACAF entered qualification.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7"><a href="#cite_note-7">[7]</a></sup> The seeding – used to draw the first four rounds of the qualifiers – was based on the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Rankings" title="FIFA World Rankings">FIFA World Rankings</a> of August 2014 (shown in parentheses).<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-approval_4-2"><a href="#cite_note-approval-4">[4]</a></sup></p>
<table class="wikitable">
<caption>From the August 2014 <a href="/wiki/FIFA_World_Rankings" title="FIFA World Rankings">FIFA World Rankings</a><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8"><a href="#cite_note-8">[8]</a></sup></caption>
<tr>
<th>Bye to fourth round<br/>
(Ranked 1st to 6th)</th>
<th>Bye to third round<br/>
(Ranked 7th to 8th)</th>
<th>Bye to second round<br/>
(Ranked 9th to 21st)</th>
<th>Competing in first round<br/>
(Ranked 22nd to 35th)</th>
</tr>

<p>The <a href="#Inter-confederation_play-offs">inter-confederation play-offs</a> are scheduled to be played between 6–14 November 2017.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9"><a href="#cite_note-9">[9]</a></sup></p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="First_round">First round</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONCACAF)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: First round">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_CONCACAF_First_Round" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – CONCACAF First Round">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – CONCACAF First Round</a></div>
<p>The draw for the first round was held on 15 January 2015, 19:40 <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Time_Zone" title="Eastern Time Zone">EST</a> (<a href="/wiki/UTC%E2%88%9205:00" title="UTC−05:00">UTC−5</a>), at the W Hotel at <a href="/wiki/Miami_Beach,_Florida" title="Miami Beach, Florida">Miami Beach, Florida</a>, United States.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-preliminary_draw_10-0"><a href="#cite_note-preliminary_draw-10">[10]</a></sup></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Second_round">Second round</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONCACAF)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Second round">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_CONCACAF_Second_Round" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – CONCACAF Second Round">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – CONCACAF Second Round</a></div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Third_round">Third round</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONCACAF)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Third round">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_CONCACAF_Third_Round" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – CONCACAF Third Round">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – CONCACAF Third Round</a></div>
<p>The draw for the third round was held as part of the 2018 FIFA World Cup Preliminary Draw on 25 July 2015, starting 18:00 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Moscow_Standard_Time" title="Moscow Standard Time">MSK</a> (<a href="/wiki/UTC%2B03:00" title="UTC+03:00">UTC+3</a>), at the Konstantinovsky Palace in <a href="/wiki/Strelna" title="Strelna">Strelna</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saint_Petersburg" title="Saint Petersburg">Saint Petersburg</a>, Russia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-draw_14-0"><a href="#cite_note-draw-14">[12]</a></sup></p>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Fourth_round">Fourth round</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONCACAF)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Fourth round">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_CONCACAF_Fourth_Round" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – CONCACAF Fourth Round">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – CONCACAF Fourth Round</a></div>
<p>The draw for the fourth round was held as part of the 2018 FIFA World Cup Preliminary Draw on 25 July 2015, starting 18:00 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Moscow_Standard_Time" title="Moscow Standard Time">MSK</a> (<a href="/wiki/UTC%2B03:00" title="UTC+03:00">UTC+3</a>), at the Konstantinovsky Palace in <a href="/wiki/Strelna" title="Strelna">Strelna</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saint_Petersburg" title="Saint Petersburg">Saint Petersburg</a>, Russia.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-draw_14-1"><a href="#cite_note-draw-14">[12]</a></sup></p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Groups">Groups</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONCACAF)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Groups">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<table class="wikitable collapsible collapsed">
<tr>
<th><a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification#Tiebreakers" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification tiebreakers</a></th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>In league format, the ranking of teams in each group is based on the following criteria (regulations Articles 20.6 and 20.7):<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-regulations_15-0"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-15">[13]</a></sup>
<ol>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Points_(association_football)" title="Points (association football)">Points</a> (3 points for a win, 1 point for a draw, 0 points for a loss)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Goal_difference" title="Goal difference">Goal difference</a></li>
<li>Goals scored</li>
<li>Points in matches between tied teams</li>
<li>Goal difference in matches between tied teams</li>
<li>Goals scored in matches between tied teams</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Away_goals_rule" title="Away goals rule">Away goals</a> scored in matches between tied teams (if the tie is only between two teams in home-and-away league format)</li>
<li>Fair play points
<ul>
<li>first yellow card: minus 1 point</li>
<li>indirect red card (second yellow card): minus 3 points</li>
<li>direct red card: minus 4 points</li>
<li>yellow card and direct red card: minus 5 points</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Drawing of lots by the FIFA Organising Committee</li>
</ol>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

Rules for classification: <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification#Tiebreakers" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification">Qualification tiebreakers</a></div>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Fifth_round">Fifth round</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONCACAF)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Fifth round">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_%E2%80%93_CONCACAF_Fifth_Round" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – CONCACAF Fifth Round">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification – CONCACAF Fifth Round</a></div>
<p>As with every World Cup qualification campaign since <a href="/wiki/1998_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONCACAF)" title="1998 FIFA World Cup qualification (CONCACAF)">1998</a>, CONCACAF is holding a six-team, home-and-away round-robin group known as the '<a href="/wiki/Hexagonal_(CONCACAF)" title="Hexagonal (CONCACAF)">Hexagonal</a>', or 'Hex', as its final and decisive round. As a result of the abolition of the February and August fixtures from the <a href="/wiki/FIFA_International_Match_Calendar" title="FIFA International Match Calendar">FIFA calendar</a>, the 'Hex' will for the first time not be contained within a single calendar year, but instead began in November 2016 and will conclude in October 2017.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-approval_4-4"><a href="#cite_note-approval-4">[4]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-si_5-1"><a href="#cite_note-si-5">[5]</a></sup></p>
<p>The draw for the fifth round (to decide the fixtures) was held on 8 July 2016, 10:00 <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Time_Zone" title="Eastern Time Zone">EDT</a> (<a href="/wiki/UTC%E2%88%9204:00" title="UTC−04:00">UTC−4</a>), at the CONCACAF headquarters in <a href="/wiki/Miami_Beach,_Florida" title="Miami Beach, Florida">Miami Beach</a>, <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">United States</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16"><a href="#cite_note-16">[14]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-17"><a href="#cite_note-17">[15]</a></sup><sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18"><a href="#cite_note-18">[16]</a></sup></p>
<table class="wikitable collapsible collapsed">
<tr>
<th><a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification#Tiebreakers" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification tiebreakers</a></th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>In league format, the ranking of teams in each group is based on the following criteria (regulations Articles 20.6 and 20.7):<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-regulations_15-1"><a href="#cite_note-regulations-15">[13]</a></sup>
<ol>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Points_(association_football)" title="Points (association football)">Points</a> (3 points for a win, 1 point for a draw, 0 points for a loss)</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Goal_difference" title="Goal difference">Goal difference</a></li>
<li>Goals scored</li>
<li>Points in matches between tied teams</li>
<li>Goal difference in matches between tied teams</li>
<li>Goals scored in matches between tied teams</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/Away_goals_rule" title="Away goals rule">Away goals</a> scored in matches between tied teams (if the tie is only between two teams in home-and-away league format)</li>
<li>Fair play points
<ul>
<li>first yellow card: minus 1 point</li>
<li>indirect red card (second yellow card): minus 3 points</li>
<li>direct red card: minus 4 points</li>
<li>yellow card and direct red card: minus 5 points</li>
</ul>
</li>
<li>Drawing of lots by the FIFA Organising Committee</li>
</ol>
</td>
</tr>
</table>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Inter-confederation_play-offs">Inter-confederation play-offs</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONCACAF)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Inter-confederation play-offs">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote" role="note">Main article: <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(inter-confederation_play-offs)" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification (inter-confederation play-offs)">2018 FIFA World Cup qualification (inter-confederation play-offs)</a></div>
<p>The draw for the inter-confederation play-offs was held as part of the 2018 FIFA World Cup Preliminary Draw on 25 July 2015, starting 18:00 <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Moscow_Standard_Time" title="Moscow Standard Time">MSK</a> (<a href="/wiki/UTC%2B03:00" title="UTC+03:00">UTC+3</a>), at the Konstantinovsky Palace in <a href="/wiki/Strelna" title="Strelna">Strelna</a>, <a href="/wiki/Saint_Petersburg" title="Saint Petersburg">Saint Petersburg</a>.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-PreliminaryDrawProcedure_19-0"><a href="#cite_note-PreliminaryDrawProcedure-19">[17]</a></sup> The fourth-placed team from CONCACAF was drawn against the fifth-placed team from AFC, with the CONCACAF team hosting the first leg.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-20"><a href="#cite_note-20">[18]</a></sup></p>
<table class="wikitable" style="text-align:center">
<tr>
<th style="text-align:right; width:250px">Team 1</th>
<th style="width:80px"><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Aggregate_score" title="Aggregate score"><abbr title="Aggregate score">Agg.</abbr></a></th>
<th style="text-align:left; width:250px">Team 2</th>
<th style="width:80px">1st leg</th>
<th style="width:80px">2nd leg</th>
</tr>
<tr>
<td style="text-align: right;">CONCACAF 4th place</td>
<td style="text-align: center;">Play-off 1</td>
<td style="text-align: left;">AFC 5th place</td>
<td style="text-align: center;"><a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(inter-confederation_play-offs)#CONCACAF_4th_place_v_AFC_5th_place" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification (inter-confederation play-offs)"><small>6 Nov '17</small></a></td>
<td style="text-align: center;"><a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(inter-confederation_play-offs)#AFC_5th_place_v_CONCACAF_4th_place" title="2018 FIFA World Cup qualification (inter-confederation play-offs)"><small>14 Nov '17</small></a></td>
</tr>
</table>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Notes">Notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=2018_FIFA_World_Cup_qualification_(CONCACAF)&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Notes">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="reflist" style="list-style-type: decimal;">
<ol class="references">
<li id="cite_note-order-11"><span class="mw-cite-backlink">^ <a href="#cite_ref-order_11-0"><sup><i><b>a</b></i></sup></a> <a href="#cite_ref-order_11-1"><sup><i><b>b</b></i></sup></a></span> <span class="reference-text">Order of legs reversed from originally published draw.</span></li>
<li id="cite_note-barbados-aruba-13"><span class="mw-cite-backlink"><b><a href="#cite_ref-barbados-aruba_13-0">^</a></b></span> <span class="reference-text">FIFA awarded Aruba a 3–0 win as a result of Barbados fielding the ineligible player <a href="/wiki/Hadan_Holligan" title="Hadan Holligan">Hadan Holligan</a>. Holligan failed to serve an automatic one match suspension for receiving two yellow cards earlier in the competition.<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-12"><a href="#cite_note-12">[11]</a></sup> The match originally ended 1–0 to Barbados.</span></li>
</ol>
</div>
